         Авторизация
        private void LoginButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            var loginWindow = new LoginWindow(_clientId);
            if (loginWindow.ShowDialog() == true && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(loginWindow.Token))
            {
                _oauthToken = loginWindow.Token;
                LoadUserProfile();
            }
        }

        private async void LoadUserProfile()
        {
            try
            {
                var json = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.commeoauth_token={_oauthToken});
                var user = JObject.Parse(json);
                UsernameText.Text = user[username].ToString()  Пользователь;
                LoginButton.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;

                var avatarUrl = user[avatar_url].ToString();
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(avatarUrl))
                    AvatarImage.Source = new BitmapImage(new Uri(avatarUrl));

                await LoadFeed();
            }
            catch { MessageBox.Show(Ошибка авторизации. Проверьте токен.); }
        }

         Лента
        private async void FeedButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) = await LoadFeed();

        private async Task LoadFeed()
        {
            try
            {
                var json = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.comstreamoauth_token={_oauthToken}&limit=20);
                var data = JObject.Parse(json);
                ParseTracks(data[collection]);
            }
            catch (Exception ex) { MessageBox.Show($Лента {ex.Message}); }
        }

         Лайки
        private async void LikesButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(_oauthToken)) return;
            try
            {
                var meJson = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.commeoauth_token={_oauthToken});
                var me = JObject.Parse(meJson);
                var userId = me[id].ToString();

                var json = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.comusers{userId}track_likesclient_id={_clientId}&oauth_token={_oauthToken}&limit=20);
                var data = JObject.Parse(json);
                ParseTracks(data[collection]);
            }
            catch (Exception ex) { MessageBox.Show($Лайки {ex.Message}); }
        }

         Плейлисты
        private async void PlaylistsButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(_oauthToken)) return;
            try
            {
                var meJson = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.commeoauth_token={_oauthToken});
                var me = JObject.Parse(meJson);
                var userId = me[id].ToString();

                var json = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.comusers{userId}playlistsclient_id={_clientId}&oauth_token={_oauthToken}&limit=20);
                var data = JObject.Parse(json);

                _tracks.Clear();
                foreach (var playlist in data[collection])
                {
                    var artwork = playlist[artwork_url].ToString()  playlist[calculated_artwork_url].ToString();
                    artwork = artwork.Replace(large, t300x300);
                    var trackCount = playlist[track_count].ToString()  0;
                    _tracks.Add(new Track
                    {
                        Id = playlist[id].ToString(),
                        Title = playlist[title].ToString(),
                        ArtistName = ${trackCount} треков,
                        ArtworkUrl = artwork,
                        Duration = 0,
                        IsPlaylist = true
                    });
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex) { MessageBox.Show($Плейлисты {ex.Message}); }
        }

         Поиск
        private DispatcherTimer _searchTimer;
        private void SearchBox_TextChanged(object sender, System.Windows.Controls.TextChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            SearchPlaceholder.Visibility = string.IsNullOrEmpty(SearchBox.Text)  Visibility.Visible  Visibility.Collapsed;
            _searchTimer.Stop();
            _searchTimer = new DispatcherTimer { Interval = TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(500) };
            _searchTimer.Tick += async (s, args) =
            {
                _searchTimer.Stop();
                await SearchTracks(SearchBox.Text);
            };
            _searchTimer.Start();
        }

        private async Task SearchTracks(string query)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(query)) return;
            try
            {
                var encoded = Uri.EscapeDataString(query);
                var json = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.comsearchtracksq={encoded}&client_id={_clientId}&limit=20);
                var data = JObject.Parse(json);
                ParseTracks(data[collection]);
            }
            catch { }
        }

        private void ParseTracks(JToken collection)
        {
            _tracks.Clear();
            if (collection == null) return;
            foreach (var item in collection)
            {
                var trackData = item[track]  item;
                if (trackData[kind].ToString() != track) continue;

                var artwork = trackData[artwork_url].ToString()  trackData[user][avatar_url].ToString();
                artwork = artwork.Replace(large, t300x300);

                _tracks.Add(new Track
                {
                    Id = trackData[id].ToString(),
                    Title = trackData[title].ToString(),
                    ArtistName = trackData[user][username].ToString(),
                    ArtworkUrl = artwork,
                    Duration = trackData[duration].ToObjectint()  0
                });
            }
        }

         Плеер
        private async void TracksList_SelectionChanged(object sender, System.Windows.Controls.SelectionChangedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (TracksList.SelectedItem is Track track)
            {
                if (track.IsPlaylist)
                    await LoadPlaylistTracks(track.Id);
                else
                    await PlayTrack(track);
            }
        }

        private async Task LoadPlaylistTracks(string playlistId)
        {
            try
            {
                var json = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.complaylists{playlistId}client_id={_clientId}&oauth_token={_oauthToken});
                var data = JObject.Parse(json);
                var tracks = data[tracks] as JArray;
                if (tracks == null) return;

                var missingIds = new Liststring();
                foreach (var t in tracks)
                {
                    if (t[title] == null  string.IsNullOrEmpty(t[title].ToString()))
                        missingIds.Add(t[id].ToString());
                }

                if (missingIds.Count  0)
                {
                    var ids = string.Join(,, missingIds);
                    var missingJson = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.comtracksids={ids}&client_id={_clientId}&oauth_token={_oauthToken});
                    var missingTracks = JArray.Parse(missingJson);
                    var missingDict = new Dictionarystring, JToken();
                    foreach (var t in missingTracks)
                        missingDict[t[id].ToString()] = t;

                    for (int i = 0; i  tracks.Count; i++)
                    {
                        var id = tracks[i][id].ToString();
                        if (missingDict.ContainsKey(id))
                            tracks[i] = missingDict[id];
                    }
                }

                ParseTracks(tracks);
            }
            catch (Exception ex) { MessageBox.Show($Ошибка {ex.Message}); }
        }

        private async Task PlayTrack(Track track)
        {
            try
            {
                _currentTrack = track;
                PlayerTitle.Text = track.Title;
                PlayerArtist.Text = track.ArtistName;

                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(track.ArtworkUrl))
                {
                    var bmp = new BitmapImage(new Uri(track.ArtworkUrl));
                    PlayerArtwork.Source = bmp;
                    BackgroundImage.Source = bmp;
                }

                string streamUrl = null;
                for (int attempt = 0; attempt  3; attempt++)
                {
                    try
                    {
                        var streamInfoJson = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.comtracks{track.Id}client_id={_clientId}&oauth_token={_oauthToken});
                        var streamInfo = JObject.Parse(streamInfoJson);
                        var media = streamInfo[media][transcodings];

                        if (media != null)
                        {
                            foreach (var t in media)
                            {
                                if (t[format][protocol].ToString() == progressive)
                                {
                                    var urlJson = await _http.GetStringAsync(${t[url]}client_id={_clientId}&oauth_token={_oauthToken});
                                    var urlData = JObject.Parse(urlJson);
                                    streamUrl = urlData[url].ToString();
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(streamUrl)) break;
                    }
                    catch { await Task.Delay(500); }
                }

                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(streamUrl)) { MessageBox.Show(Трек недоступен); return; }

                StopPlayback();
                await Task.Delay(100);

                _audioReader = new MediaFoundationReader(streamUrl);
                _wavePlayer = new WaveOutEvent();
                _wavePlayer.Init(_audioReader);
                _wavePlayer.Volume = (float)(VolumeSlider.Value  100);
                _wavePlayer.PlaybackStopped += async (s, args) =
                {
                    if (args.Exception == null && _isPlaying)
                    {
                        await Dispatcher.InvokeAsync(() =
                        {
                            var idx = TracksList.SelectedIndex;
                            if (idx  _tracks.Count - 1)
                                TracksList.SelectedIndex = idx + 1;
                        });
                    }
                };
                _wavePlayer.Play();
                _isPlaying = true;
                PlayPauseButton.Content = ⏸;
                ProgressSlider.Maximum = _audioReader.TotalTime.TotalSeconds;
                _progressTimer.Start();
            }
            catch (Exception ex) { MessageBox.Show($Ошибка воспроизведения {ex.Message}); }
        }

        private void StopPlayback()
        {
            _progressTimer.Stop();
            _wavePlayer.Stop();
            _wavePlayer.Dispose();
            _audioReader.Dispose();
            _wavePlayer = null;
            _audioReader = null;
            _isPlaying = false;
        }

        private void PlayPauseButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (_wavePlayer == null) return;
            if (_isPlaying) { _wavePlayer.Pause(); PlayPauseButton.Content = ▶; }
            else { _wavePlayer.Play(); PlayPauseButton.Content = ⏸; }
            _isPlaying = !_isPlaying;
        }

        private void PrevButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            var idx = TracksList.SelectedIndex;
            if (idx  0) TracksList.SelectedIndex = idx - 1;
        }

        private void NextButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            var idx = TracksList.SelectedIndex;
            if (idx  _tracks.Count - 1) TracksList.SelectedIndex = idx + 1;
        }

        private void VolumeSlider_ValueChanged(object sender, RoutedPropertyChangedEventArgsdouble e)
        {
            if (_wavePlayer != null)
                _wavePlayer.Volume = (float)(e.NewValue  100);
        }

        private void ProgressSlider_PreviewMouseDown(object sender, MouseButtonEventArgs e)
        {
            _isDragging = true;
        }

        private void ProgressSlider_PreviewMouseUp(object sender, MouseButtonEventArgs e)
        {
            _isDragging = false;
            if (_audioReader != null)
                _audioReader.CurrentTime = TimeSpan.FromSeconds(ProgressSlider.Value);
        }

        private void ProgressTimer_Tick(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
            if (_audioReader != null && !_isDragging)
            {
                ProgressSlider.Value = _audioReader.CurrentTime.TotalSeconds;
                CurrentTimeText.Text = _audioReader.CurrentTime.ToString(@mss);
                TotalTimeText.Text = _audioReader.TotalTime.ToString(@mss);
            }
        }

        private async void LikeTrack_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (TracksList.SelectedItem is not Track track  track.IsPlaylist) return;
            MessageBox.Show(Лайки недоступны без официального API ключа);
        }

        private async void AddToPlaylist_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            if (TracksList.SelectedItem is not Track track  track.IsPlaylist) return;
            try
            {
                var meJson = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.commeoauth_token={_oauthToken});
                var me = JObject.Parse(meJson);
                var userId = me[id].ToString();

                var json = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.comusers{userId}playlistsclient_id={_clientId}&oauth_token={_oauthToken}&limit=50);
                var data = JObject.Parse(json);
                var playlists = data[collection] as JArray;
                if (playlists == null  !playlists.HasValues) { MessageBox.Show(Нет плейлистов); return; }

                var dialog = new PlaylistPickerDialog(playlists);
                if (dialog.ShowDialog() != true) return;
                var selectedPlaylist = dialog.SelectedPlaylist;

                var playlistJson = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.complaylists{selectedPlaylist[id]}client_id={_clientId}&oauth_token={_oauthToken});
                var playlistData = JObject.Parse(playlistJson);
                var existingTracks = playlistData[tracks] as JArray;

                if (existingTracks != null && existingTracks.Any(t = t[id].ToString() == track.Id))
                {
                    MessageBox.Show(⚠️ Этот трек уже есть в плейлисте!);
                    return;
                }

                var trackIds = existingTracks.Select(t = new JObject { [id] = t[id].ToObjectlong() }).ToList()  new ListJObject();
                trackIds.Add(new JObject { [id] = long.Parse(track.Id) });

                var body = new JObject { [playlist] = new JObject { [tracks] = new JArray(trackIds) } };
                var content = new StringContent(body.ToString(), System.Text.Encoding.UTF8, applicationjson);
                var putRequest = new HttpRequestMessage(HttpMethod.Put,
                    $httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.complaylists{selectedPlaylist[id]}client_id={_clientId}&oauth_token={_oauthToken});
                putRequest.Content = content;
                var response = await _http.SendAsync(putRequest);

                if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
                    MessageBox.Show($✅ Трек добавлен в {selectedPlaylist[title]}!);
                else
                    MessageBox.Show($Ошибка {response.StatusCode});
            }
            catch (Exception ex) { MessageBox.Show($Ошибка {ex.Message}); }
        }

        private void SpotifyImportButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            var window = new CsvImportWindow(_clientId, _oauthToken);
            window.ShowDialog();
        }
    }

private void ScrollViewer_PreviewMouseWheel(object sender, MouseWheelEventArgs e)
{
    var sv = sender as ScrollViewer;
    sv.ScrollToVerticalOffset(sv.VerticalOffset - e.Delta  3.0);
    e.Handled = true;
}

Вставь в SettingsWindow.xaml.cs

csharp
using System.Windows;
using System.Windows.Media;

namespace SoundCloudClient
{
    public partial class SettingsWindow  Window
    {
        public Color Color1 { get; private set; } = Color.FromRgb(13, 13, 13);
        public Color Color2 { get; private set; } = Color.FromRgb(26, 26, 46);
        public Color Color3 { get; private set; } = Color.FromRgb(13, 13, 13);

        public SettingsWindow()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
        }

        private void SetPreview(Color c1, Color c2, Color c3)
        {
            Color1 = c1; Color2 = c2; Color3 = c3;
            PreviewStop1.Color = c1;
            PreviewStop2.Color = c2;
            PreviewStop3.Color = c3;
        }

        private void Dark_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) =
            SetPreview(Color.FromRgb(13,13,13), Color.FromRgb(26,26,26), Color.FromRgb(13,13,13));

        private void Blue_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) =
            SetPreview(Color.FromRgb(10,10,30), Color.FromRgb(26,26,78), Color.FromRgb(10,10,30));

        private void Purple_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) =
            SetPreview(Color.FromRgb(15,5,30), Color.FromRgb(45,27,105), Color.FromRgb(15,5,30));

        private void Green_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) =
            SetPreview(Color.FromRgb(5,20,10), Color.FromRgb(13,43,26), Color.FromRgb(5,20,10));

        private void Red_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) =
            SetPreview(Color.FromRgb(20,5,5), Color.FromRgb(43,13,13), Color.FromRgb(20,5,5));

        private void Orange_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) =
            SetPreview(Color.FromRgb(20,10,0), Color.FromRgb(43,21,0), Color.FromRgb(20,10,0));

        private void ApplyButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
        {
            DialogResult = true;
            Close();
        }
    }
}
И в MainWindow.xaml.cs замени SettingsButton_Click

csharp
private void SettingsButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
{
    var settings = new SettingsWindow();
    if (settings.ShowDialog() == true)
    {
         Применяем градиент к главному окну
        var border = (System.Windows.Controls.Border)Content;
        var brush = new LinearGradientBrush();
        brush.StartPoint = new System.Windows.Point(0, 0);
        brush.EndPoint = new System.Windows.Point(1, 1);
        brush.GradientStops.Add(new GradientStop(settings.Color1, 0));
        brush.GradientStops.Add(new GradientStop(settings.Color2, 0.5));
        brush.GradientStops.Add(new GradientStop(settings.Color3, 1));
        border.Background = brush;
    }
}

Сначала в MainWindow.xaml.cs исправь MaximizeButton_Click

csharp
private void MaximizeButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
{
    if (WindowState == WindowState.Maximized)
    {
        WindowState = WindowState.Normal;
        MaximizeButton.Content = □;
        Margin = new Thickness(0);
    }
    else
    {
        WindowState = WindowState.Maximized;
        MaximizeButton.Content = ❐;
        Margin = new Thickness(7);
    }
}
И добавь анимацию сворачивания — замени MinimizeButton_Click

csharp
private void MinimizeButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
{
    var anim = new System.Windows.Media.Animation.DoubleAnimation
    {
        To = 0,
        Duration = TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(200),
        EasingFunction = new System.Windows.Media.Animation.QuadraticEase()
    };
    anim.Completed += (s, args) = WindowState = WindowState.Minimized;
    BeginAnimation(OpacityProperty, anim);
}

protected override void OnStateChanged(EventArgs e)
{
    base.OnStateChanged(e);
    if (WindowState == WindowState.Normal)
    {
        var anim = new System.Windows.Media.Animation.DoubleAnimation
        {
            To = 1,
            Duration = TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(200)
        };
        BeginAnimation(OpacityProperty, anim);
    }
}

Теперь сохранение токена. В MainWindow.xaml.cs добавь два метода и вызов в конструкторе

csharp
private void SaveToken(string token)
{
    try
    {
        var folder = System.IO.Path.Combine(
            Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.LocalApplicationData),
            SoundCloudDesktop);
        System.IO.Directory.CreateDirectory(folder);
        var file = System.IO.Path.Combine(folder, session.dat);
        System.IO.File.WriteAllText(file, token);
    }
    catch { }
}

private string LoadToken()
{
    try
    {
        var file = System.IO.Path.Combine(
            Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.LocalApplicationData),
            SoundCloudDesktop, session.dat);
        if (System.IO.File.Exists(file))
            return System.IO.File.ReadAllText(file).Trim();
    }
    catch { }
    return null;
}
В конструкторе MainWindow() добавь в конец

csharp
 Автовход
var savedToken = LoadToken();

private void LoginButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
{
    var loginWindow = new LoginWindow(_clientId);
    if (loginWindow.ShowDialog() == true && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(loginWindow.Token))
    {
        _oauthToken = loginWindow.Token;
        SaveToken(_oauthToken);
        LoadUserProfile();
    }

Теперь в MainWindow.xaml.cs замени PlayPauseButton_Click чтобы переключал иконки

csharp
private void PlayPauseButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
{
    if (_wavePlayer == null) return;

    var template = PlayPauseButton.Template;
    var playIcon = (System.Windows.Shapes.Path)template.FindName(PlayIcon, PlayPauseButton);
    var pauseIcon = (System.Windows.Controls.StackPanel)template.FindName(PauseIcon, PlayPauseButton);

    if (_isPlaying)
    {
        _wavePlayer.Pause();
        if (playIcon != null) playIcon.Visibility = Visibility.Visible;
        if (pauseIcon != null) pauseIcon.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;
    }
    else
    {
        _wavePlayer.Play();
        if (playIcon != null) playIcon.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;
        if (pauseIcon != null) pauseIcon.Visibility = Visibility.Visible;
    }
    _isPlaying = !_isPlaying;
}

        Dispatcher.InvokeAsync(() =
        {
            PlayPauseButton.ApplyTemplate();
            var playIcon = PlayPauseButton.Template.FindName(PlayIcon, PlayPauseButton) as System.Windows.Shapes.Path;
            var pauseIcon = PlayPauseButton.Template.FindName(PauseIcon, PlayPauseButton) as System.Windows.Controls.StackPanel;
            if (playIcon != null) playIcon.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;
            if (pauseIcon != null) pauseIcon.Visibility = Visibility.Visible;
        });
        ProgressSlider.Maximum = _audioReader.TotalTime.TotalSeconds;
        _progressTimer.Start();
    }
    catch (Exception ex) { MessageBox.Show($Ошибка воспроизведения {ex.Message}); }
}

private void StopPlayback()
{
    _progressTimer.Stop();
    _wavePlayer.Stop();
    _wavePlayer.Dispose();
    _audioReader.Dispose();
    _wavePlayer = null;
    _audioReader = null;
    _isPlaying = false;
}



private void PrevButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
{
    var idx = TracksList.SelectedIndex;
    if (idx  0) TracksList.SelectedIndex = idx - 1;
}

private void NextButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
{
    var idx = TracksList.SelectedIndex;
    if (idx  _tracks.Count - 1) TracksList.SelectedIndex = idx + 1;
}

private void VolumeSlider_ValueChanged(object sender, RoutedPropertyChangedEventArgsdouble e)
{
    if (_wavePlayer != null)
        _wavePlayer.Volume = (float)(e.NewValue  100);
}

private void ProgressSlider_PreviewMouseDown(object sender, MouseButtonEventArgs e)
{
    _isDragging = true;
}

private void ProgressSlider_PreviewMouseUp(object sender, MouseButtonEventArgs e)
{
    _isDragging = false;
    if (_audioReader != null)
        _audioReader.CurrentTime = TimeSpan.FromSeconds(ProgressSlider.Value);
}

private void ProgressTimer_Tick(object sender, EventArgs e)
{
    if (_audioReader != null && !_isDragging)
    {
        ProgressSlider.Value = _audioReader.CurrentTime.TotalSeconds;
        CurrentTimeText.Text = _audioReader.CurrentTime.ToString(@mss);
        TotalTimeText.Text = _audioReader.TotalTime.ToString(@mss);
    }
}

private async void LikeTrack_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
{
    if (TracksList.SelectedItem is not Track track  track.IsPlaylist) return;
    MessageBox.Show(Лайки недоступны без официального API ключа);
}

csharp
private async void PlaylistsButton_Click(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)
{
    if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(_oauthToken)) return;
    try
    {
        var meJson = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.commeoauth_token={_oauthToken});
        var me = JObject.Parse(meJson);
        var userId = me[id].ToString();

        var json = await _http.GetStringAsync($httpsapi-v2.soundcloud.comusers{userId}playlistsclient_id={_clientId}&oauth_token={_oauthToken}&limit=20);
        var data = JObject.Parse(json);

        _tracks.Clear();
        foreach (var playlist in data[collection])
        {
            var artwork = playlist[artwork_url].ToString()  playlist[calculated_artwork_url].ToString();
            artwork = artwork.Replace(large, t300x300);
            var trackCount = playlist[track_count].ToString()  0;
            _tracks.Add(new Track
            {
                Id = playlist[id].ToString(),
                Title = playlist[title].ToString(),
                ArtistName = ${trackCount} треков,
                ArtworkUrl = artwork,
                Duration = 0,
                IsPlaylist = true
            });
        }
    }
    catch (Exception ex) { MessageBox.Show($Плейлисты {ex.Message}); }
}

Claude responded Честно — без официального API ключа от SoundCloud это невозможно.
Честно — без официального API ключа от SoundCloud это невозможно. Они заблокировали созданиередактирование плейлистов, лайки и другие функции для неофициальных приложений.

Варианты

Ждать одобрения заявки — ты отправлял письмо на api@soundcloud.com. Если одобрят — все функции заработают.
Spotify клиент — у Spotify API лучше, но нужен Premium для разработчика (~10$мес). Зато все функции будут работать.
Просто использовать официальное приложение 😄

26 апр.
Claude responded Из музыкальных сервисов с открытым API
Из музыкальных сервисов с открытым API

Deezer — бесплатный API, можно всё плейлисты, лайки, поиск, стриминг. Регистрация приложения бесплатная и без одобрения.

YouTube Music — unofficially через ytmusicapi, но это не официальный API.

Last.fm — только история и рекомендации, стриминга нет.

Spotify — всё есть но нужен Premium для разработчика.

Я бы рекомендовал Deezer — регистрируешься на developers.deezer.com, получаешь ключ сразу, и всё работает бесплатно. Библиотека треков огромная.
